<div><br>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">TOA Distribution Systems Inc</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">(formerly known as Skyhigh Resources Inc)</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">Notes to Financial Statements</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">June 30, 2016</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times 
New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">NOTE 1.</font><font 
id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 
5.14pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, 
serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">BASIS OF PRESENTATION</font></div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">In August 2009 the Company initiated a number of corporate 
changes, including 1), a name change to TOA Distribution Systems Inc, (formerly 
known as Skyhigh Resources Inc, 2) approved a 10 for 1 roll forward of its 
issued and outstanding common stock, 3), increased it authorized par value 
$0.001 common shares to 250,000,000 shares (formerly 50,000,000), and 4), 
authorized 10,000,000 par value $0.001 preferred shares.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">In mid-2009, the Company resolved to change its corporate focus, 
moving from mining and exploration into bottled drinking water 
distribution.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">The Company owned two (2) mineral properties acquired from related 
parties in January 2008 by issuing stock to related parties. The purchase price 
was fully impaired. In February 2012 these claims were deemed surplus and were 
sold in May 2012.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">On September 2, 2009 the Company entered into to a Sub-Distribution
agreement with Taste of Aruba (US), Inc to distribute bottled water products 
produced in Aruba by Taste of Aruba-Premium Aruban Water.&#160;&#160; The 
territory in which the Company can distribute these products include the United 
States and all its territories and insular areas in the Caribbean and Pacific 
such as but not limited to Puerto Rico, U.S. Virgin Islands, Marshall Islands, 
and Guam, and all of Canada.&#160; In January 2016, the Company and Taste of 
Aruba agreed to cancel the Sub-Distribution agreement on a no loss no gain basis
for either party. Taste of Aruba was unable to confirm when its products would 
be available for resale. The 17,000,000 shares issued to cover the cost of the 
Sub-Distribution Agreement have been returned and were cancelled on January18, 
2016. This transaction which included full impairment has been reversed in the 
financial records for the year ended March 31, 2016.</div>
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New 
Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 6pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE:
10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">In the opinion of 
management, the accompanying balance sheets and related statements of income, 
cash flows, and stockholders' equity include all adjustments, consisting only of
normal recurring items, necessary for their fair presentation in conformity with
accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America ("U.S. 
GAAP"). Preparing financial statements requires management to make estimates and
assumptions that affect the reported amounts of assets, liabilities, revenue, 
and expenses. Actual results and outcomes may differ from management's estimates
and assumptions</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New 
Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">.</font></div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 
'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">NOTE 2.</font><font 
id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 
5.14pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, 
serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">GOING CONCERN</font></div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">The accompanying financial statements have been prepared in 
conformity with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) in the United 
States of America, which contemplates continuation of the Company as a going 
concern. &#160;However, the Company has no business operations to date, 
accumulated losses amounting to $174,401 and must secure additional financing to
commence the Company's plan of operations, which means there is substantial 
concern about the Company's ability to continue as a going concern. &#160;The
Company intends to acquire additional operating capital through equity offerings
to the public to fund its business plan or loans from shareholders and others. 
There is no assurance that the equity offerings will be successful or loans will
be received to provide sufficient funds to commence operations or to assure the 
eventual profitability of the Company.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 
'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">NOTE 3.</font><font 
id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 
5.14pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, 
serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">SUB-DISTRIBUTION AGREEMENT</font></div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">On September 2, 2009 the Company signed an Exclusive Sub-
Distribution Agreement ("Agreement") with Taste of Aruba (US) Inc, a State of 
Nevada Incorporated company, owner and master distributor of products from Taste
of Aruba-Premium Aruban Water. Under the Agreement, the Company will distribute 
in the United States, its territories and insular areas in the Caribbean and 
Pacific and Canada, bottled water produced under license in Aruba by Water 
Energy Company-Aruba.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">In January 2016, the Company and Taste of Aruba agreed to cancel 
the Sub-Distribution agreement on a no loss no gain basis for either party. 
Taste of Aruba was unable to confirm when its products would be available for 
resale. The 17,000,000 shares issued to cover the cost of the Sub-Distribution 
Agreement have been returned and were cancelled on January18, 2016. This 
transaction which included full impairment has been reversed in the financial 
records for the year ended March 31, 2016.</div>
<div><br>
</div>

10pt">

<div><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif;

&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#

serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">LOANS PAYABLE</font></div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">Loans payable to related parties, were received from a director 
of the Company and others closely associated persons or businesses. These funds 
were provided as cash loans to cover operating expenses and as payment for 
services provided.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">Loans payable to the past and current presidents totaled $6,214 
made up of principal amounting to $3,742 and accrued interest of $2,472</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">Loans payable to a closely associated business totaled 88,937 
made up of principal amounting to $75,498 and accrued interest amounting to 
$13,439.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">In aggregate, Loans Payable Related Parties to June 30, 2016 
totaled $95,151 made up of $79,240 for principal and $15,911 for accrued 
interest.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times 
New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">NOTE 7.</font><font 
id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 
5.14pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, 
serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">EQUITY</font></div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">At a special shareholders meeting held August 13, 2009, the 
shareholders approved the change of the Company's name to TOA Distribution 
Systems Inc, approved charges to the authorized capital which included creation 
of 10,000,000 shares of preferred stock at a par value of $0.01 per share and 
increased the authorized common stock to 250,000,000 with a par value of $0.001 
per share. As well, the shareholders approved a 10 for 1 forward stock split of 
the outstanding shares. All share amounts shown in these financial statements 
have been adjusted retroactively to account for the forward stock split.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">At <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman',
Times, serif">June 30, 2016 </font>we had zero preferred stock issued and 
outstanding and had 30,100,060 common shares issued and outstanding, which were 
issued on the dates and purposes listed below.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt">-&#160; 15,000,000 common shares issued to a 
director for cash at $0.0001 on December 13, 2007</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt">-&#160; 600,000 common shares issued for 
services at $0.0025 on December 13, 2007</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt">-&#160; 2,000,000 common shares issued for a 
mining property at $0.01 on January10, 2007</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt">-&#160; 2,400,000 common shares issued for 
cash on May 11, 2009</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt">-&#160; 4,285,000 common shares issued for 
accounts payable on June 1, 2009</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;-&#160; 3,315,000 
common shares issued to a related party for loan payable on June 13, 2009</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt">-&#160; 2,500,000 common shares issued for a 
mining property on June 15, 2009</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt">-&#160; 17,000,000 common shares issued for a
sub-distribution agreement on Sept 2, 2009</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 18pt">- (17,000,000) common shares returned for 
cancelled sub-distribution agreement January18, 2016</div>
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt"><font 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-
WEIGHT: bold">NOTE 8.</font><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 
5.14pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#
160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, 
serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">CONTRIBUTED SURPLUS</font></div>
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New 
Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">The Company owned two 
(2) mineral claims that had been deemed surplus and fully impaired. On May 1, 
2012 these claims were sold to a related party to whom the Company had loans 
payable. The terms of the sale was a reduction of the loans payable and 
proportionate accrued interest in aggregate amounting to Twenty-Five Thousand 
Dollar, ($25,000.00), an extension on the due date of these loan payable, a 
reduction of the rate of interest payable from 10% to 5% and the issuance by the
purchaser, of shares in its two private companies. The Company elected to 
distribute these private company shares equally to the Company's shareholders. 
As these shares were valued at $0 by the Company there was no impact on the 
financial statements.<br>
</div>

Companies to adopt these guidelines earlier</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-

the financial statements were issued. There were no significant subsequent 
events that need to be disclosed.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">ITEM 2: MANAGEMENT'S DISCUSSION AND ANALYSIS OR PLAN OF 
OPERATION</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">PLAN OF OPERATION</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">In an effort to make available the facilities of the public market 
to our funding requirements, the Company intends to make application to FINRA 
for a trading symbol. The Company's application to FINRA will consist of current
corporate information, financial statements and other documents as required by 
Rule 15c211 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934.</div>
<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New 
Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt">On November 17, 
2012, the Company filed a Form 8-K, Item 5.02: Departure of Directors or Certain
Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers with the 
Securities and Exchange Commission. This 8-K filing disclosed the resignation of
Trevor Blank as a Director and from all officer positions held with the Company.
Concurrent with Mr. Blank's resignation, Mr. Andy Ruppanner was appointed to 
serve as sole director and as President and CEO, Vice-President and CFO, 
Secretary and Treasurer.</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">In January 2016 the Company's and Taste of Aruba mutually agreed to
cancel their Sub-Distribution Agreement.&#160; Taste of Aruba was unable to 
confirm when its products would be available for resale. The cancelation 
agreement was on the basis of a no loss, no gain for either party. The 
17,000,000 shares issued as the cost for the Sub-Distribution Agreement have 
been returned and cancelled.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">Subsequent to the period ending June 30, 2016, the Company entered 
into discussion with another non related entity to obtain a license for a water 
treatment technology</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">RESULTS OF OPERATIONS</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-
WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">Interim Periods:</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">No sales or income was recorded for the period ended June 30, 
2016</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-
WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 
'Times New Roman', Times, serif">Operating Costs and Expenses for the three 
month period ended June 30, 2016</font> compared to the same period ended in 
2015.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-
WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 
'Times New Roman', Times, serif">For the three-month period ended </font>at June
30, 2016 compared to the same period ended in 2015.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">Net losses incurred during the three-month period ending June 30, 
2016<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, 
serif">&#160;</font>were $3,479 a decrease of $1,028 compared to $4,507 amount 
for the same period ended June 30, 2015.</div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left"><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">General administrative expenses for three-months ended June 30, 
2016 were $2,460 compared to $3,591, in the June 30, 2015 period, a decrease of 
$1,131 made up primarily by a changed method of recording accrued 
expenses.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">Interest cost June 30, 2016 increased by $103, as a result of the 
larger loan principal amount upon which interest was calculated.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">LIQUIDITY AND CAPITAL RESOURCES</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">Our cash balance was nil on June 30, 2016. During this three 
month period ended June 30, 2016<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 
'Times New Roman', Times, serif">&#160;</font>we received loans from related 
parties amounting to $2,460 and have a commitment for any additional funds 
required to fund our limited levels of operations through March 31, 2017. We 
have not generated any revenue to date.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">We have loans payable including interest amounting to $95,150 
due June 30, 2016.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">Our auditor has issued a going concern opinion. This means that 
there is substantial doubt that we can continue as an on-going business for the 
next twelve months unless we obtain additional capital to pay our bills. This is
because we have not generated revenues and no revenues are anticipated until we 
begin receiving and selling water products. There is no assurance we will ever 
reach that stage.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">OFF-BALANCE SHEET ARRANGEMENTS</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: justify">We have no off-balance sheet arrangements that have or are 
reasonably likely to have a current or future effect on our financial condition,
changes in financial condition, revenues or expenses, results of operations, 
liquidity, capital expenditures or capital resources.</div>
<div><br>

serif">CONTROLS AND PROCEDURES</font></div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">EVALUATION OF DISCLOSURE CONTROLS</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">As of the end of the period covered by this report, we conducted an
evaluation, under the supervision and with the participation of our chief 
executive officer and chief financial officer, of our disclosure controls and 
procedures (as defined in Rule 13a-15(e) of the Exchange Act). Based upon this 
evaluation, our chief executive officer and chief financial officer concluded 
that our disclosure controls and procedures are ineffective to ensure that 
information required to be disclosed by us in the reports that we file or submit
under the Exchange Act is recorded, processed, summarized and reported, within 
the time periods specified in the Security and Exchange Commission's rules and 
forms.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">There has been no change in our internal control over financial 
reporting during the current quarter that has materially affected, or is 
reasonably likely to materially affect, our internal control over financial 
reporting.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">EVALUATION OF AND REPORT ON INTERNAL CONTROL OVER FINANCIAL 
REPORTING</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">Our management is responsible for establishing and maintaining 
adequate internal control over financial reporting for&#160; the&#160; 
company.&#160; Internal&#160; control&#160; over financial reporting is to 
provide reasonable assurance regarding the reliability of our&#160; 
financial&#160; reporting&#160; purposes&#160; accordance&#160; with&#160; 
accounting&#160; principles generally&#160; accepted in the United&#160; States 
of&#160; America.&#160; Internal&#160; control&#160; over financial&#160; 
reporting&#160; includes&#160; maintaining&#160; records that in&#160; 
reasonable&#160; detail accurately and fairly reflect our transaction;&#160; 
providing&#160; reasonable&#160; assurance that&#160; transactions&#160; are 
recorded as necessary for&#160; preparations of our financial statements;&#160; 
providing&#160; reasonable assurance that receipts and&#160; expenditures of 
company&#160; assets&#160; are&#160; made in&#160; accordance&#160; with&#160; 
management&#160; authorization;&#160; and providing&#160;&#160; 
reasonable&#160;&#160; assurance&#160; that&#160; unauthorized&#160;&#160;
acquisitions,&#160;&#160; use&#160; or disposition of company assets that could 
have a material effect on our financial statements would be prevented or 
detected.</div>
<div><br>
</div>
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-
ALIGN: left">Management conducted an evaluation of the effectiveness of our 
internal control over financial reporting based on the framework in Internal 
Control &#8211; Integrated Framework issued by the Committee of Sponsoring 
Organizations of the Treadway Commission.&#160; Based on this evaluation 
management concluded that the Company's internal control over financial 
reporting was ineffective as of June 30, 2016. There were no changes in our 
internal controls over financial reporting during the period&#160; ended&#160; 
June 30, 2016 that have&#160; materially&#160; affected,&#160; or are 
reasonable&#160; likely to materially&#160; affect our internal control over 
financial reporting.</div>

    <us-gaap:BasisOfPresentationAndSignificantAccountingPoliciesTextBlock 
contextRef="From2016-04-01to2016-06-30">&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman,
Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 
1.&amp;#9;BASIS OF PRESENTATION&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 
10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify"&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"&gt;In August 2009 the 
Company initiated a&#13;number of corporate changes, including 1), a name change
to TOA Distribution Systems Inc, (formerly known as Skyhigh Resources&#13;Inc, 
2) approved a 10 for 1 roll forward of its issued and outstanding common stock, 
3), increased it authorized par value $0.001&#13;common shares to 250,000,000 
shares (formerly 50,000,000), and 4), authorized 10,000,000 par value $0.001 
preferred shares.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, 
Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify"&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"&gt;In mid-2009, the 
Company resolved to change its corporate focus,&#13;moving from mining and 
exploration into bottled drinking water distribution.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p 
style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify"&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New 
Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"&gt;The Company owned 
two (2) mineral properties acquired from related&#13;parties in January 2008 by 
issuing stock to related parties. The purchase price was fully impaired. In 
February 2012 these claims&#13;were deemed surplus and were sold in May 
2012.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; 
margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p 
style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify"&gt;On September 2, 2009 the Company entered into to a Sub-
Distribution&#13;agreement with Taste of Aruba (US), Inc to distribute bottled 
water products produced in Aruba by Taste of Aruba-Premium Aruban&#13;Water. The
territory in which the Company can distribute these products include the United 
States and all its territories and insular&#13;areas in the Caribbean and 
Pacific such as but not limited to Puerto Rico, U.S. Virgin Islands, Marshall 
Islands, and Guam, and&#13;all of Canada. In January 2016, the Company and Taste
of Aruba agreed to cancel the Sub-Distribution agreement on a no loss 
no&#13;gain basis for either party. Taste of Aruba was unable to confirm when 
its products would be available for resale. The 17,000,000&#13;shares issued to 
cover the cost of the Sub-Distribution Agreement have been returned and were 
cancelled on January18, 2016. This&#13;transaction which included full 
impairment has been reversed in the financial records for the year ended March 
31, 2016.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, 
Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"&gt;In the opinion of management, the 
accompanying balance sheets&#13;and related statements of income, cash flows, 
and stockholders' equity include all adjustments, consisting only of normal 
recurring&#13;items, necessary for their fair presentation in conformity with 
accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of&#13;America
(&amp;#34;U.S. GAAP&amp;#34;). Preparing financial statements requires 
management to make estimates and assumptions that affect&#13;the reported 
amounts of assets, liabilities, revenue, and expenses. Actual results and 
outcomes may differ from management's estimates&#13;and assumptions&lt;b&gt;. 
&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</us-
gaap:BasisOfPresentationAndSignificantAccountingPoliciesTextBlock>

&amp;#160;However, the Company has no business operations to date, accumulated 
losses&#13;amounting to $174,401 and must secure additional financing to 
commence the Company&amp;#146;s plan of operations, which means there&#13;is 
substantial concern about the Company&amp;#146;s ability to continue as a going 
concern. &amp;#160;The Company intends to acquire additional&#13;operating 
capital through equity offerings to the public to fund its business plan or 
loans from shareholders and others. There&#13;is no assurance that the equity 
offerings will be successful or loans will be received to provide sufficient 
funds to commence&#13;operations or to assure the eventual profitability of the

0.25in"&gt;- 2,500,000 common&#13;shares issued for a mining property on June 
15, 2009&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times,
Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in"&gt;- 17,000,000 
common&#13;shares issued for a sub-distribution agreement on Sept 2, 
2009&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif;

shares&#13;returned for cancelled sub-distribution agreement January18,

    <TOAD:ContributedSurplusTextBlock contextRef="From2016-04-01to2016-06-
30">&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-
align: justify"&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 8.&amp;#9;CONTRIBUTED 
SURPLUS&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, 
Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"&gt;The Company owned two (2) 
mineral claims that had been deemed&#13;surplus and fully impaired. On May 1, 
2012 these claims were sold to a related party to whom the Company had loans 
payable. The&#13;terms of the sale was a reduction of the loans payable and 
proportionate accrued interest in aggregate amounting to Twenty-
Five&#13;Thousand Dollar, ($25,000.00), an extension on the due date of these 
loan payable, a reduction of the rate of interest payable&#13;from 10% to 5% and
the issuance by the purchaser, of shares in its two private companies. The 
Company elected to distribute these&#13;private company shares equally to the 
Company&amp;#146;s shareholders. As these shares were valued at $0 by the 
Company there was&#13;no impact on the financial 
statements.&lt;/p&gt;</TOAD:ContributedSurplusTextBlock>

<tr><td><div class="body" style="padding: 2px;">
<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="top.Show.toggleNext( this );">- 
Definition</a><div><p>Carrying value as of the balance sheet date of obligations
incurred and payable, pertaining to costs that are statutory in nature, are 
incurred on contractual obligations, or accumulate over time and for which 
invoices have not yet been received or will not be rendered. Examples include 
taxes, interest, rent and utilities. Used to reflect the current portion of the 
liabilities (due within one year or within the normal operating cycle if 
longer).</p></div>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="authRefData" 
style="display: none;" id="defref_us-gaap_AdditionalPaidInCapital">
<tr><td class="hide"><a style="color: white;" href="javascript:void(0);" 
onclick="top.Show.hideAR();">X</a></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="body" style="padding: 2px;">
<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="top.Show.toggleNext( this );">- 
Definition</a><div><p>Excess of issue price over par or stated value of the 
entity's capital stock and amounts received from other transactions involving 
the entity's stock or stockholders. Includes adjustments to additional paid in 
capital. Some examples of such adjustments include recording the issuance of 
debt with a beneficial conversion feature and certain tax consequences of equity
instruments awarded to employees. Use this element for the aggregate amount of 
additional paid-in capital associated with common and preferred stock. For 
additional paid-in capital associated with only common stock, use the element 
additional paid in capital, common stock. For additional paid-in capital 
associated with only preferred stock, use the element additional paid in 
capital, preferred stock.</p></div>

Definition</a><div><p>Sum of the carrying amounts as of the balance sheet date 
of all assets that are expected to be realized in cash, sold, or consumed within
one year (or the normal operating cycle, if longer). Assets are probable future 
economic benefits obtained or controlled by an entity as a result of past 
transactions or events.</p></div>

<tr><td><div class="body" style="padding: 2px;">
<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="top.Show.toggleNext( this );">- 
Definition</a><div><p>Total of all stockholders' equity (deficit) items, net of 
receivables from officers, directors, owners, and affiliates of the entity which
are attributable to the parent. The amount of the economic entity's 
stockholders' equity attributable to the parent excludes the amount of 
stockholders' equity which is allocable to that ownership interest in subsidiary
equity which is not attributable to the parent (noncontrolling interest, 
minority interest). This excludes temporary equity and is sometimes called 
permanent equity.</p></div>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="authRefData"

<tr><td class="hide"><a style="color: white;" href="javascript:void(0);" 
onclick="top.Show.hideAR();">X</a></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="body" style="padding: 2px;">
<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="top.Show.toggleNext( this );">- 
Definition</a><div><p>The amount of net income or loss for the period per each 
share in instances when basic and diluted earnings per share are the same amount
and reported as a single line item on the face of the financial statements.  
Basic earnings per share is the amount of net income or loss for the period per 
each share of common stock or unit outstanding during the reporting period.  
Diluted earnings per share includes the amount of net income or loss for the 
period available to each share of common stock or common unit outstanding during
the reporting period and to each share or unit that would have been outstanding 
assuming the issuance of common shares or units for all dilutive potential 
common shares or units outstanding during the reporting period.</p></div>
<a href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="top.Show.toggleNext( this );">+ 
References</a><div style="display: none;"><p>No definition available.</p></div>

<th class="tl" colspan="1" rowspan="2"><div style="width: 200px;"><strong>BASIS 
OF PRESENTATION<br></strong></div></th>
<th class="th" colspan="1">3 Months Ended</th>
</tr>
<tr><th class="th"><div>Jun. 30, 2016</div></th></tr>
<tr class="re">
<td class="pl " style="border-bottom: 0px;" valign="top"><a class="a" 
href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="top.Show.showAR( this, 'defref_us-
gaap_AccountingPoliciesAbstract', window );"><strong>Accounting Policies 
[Abstract]</strong></a></td>
<td class="text">&#160;<span></span>
</td>
</tr>
<tr class="ro">
<td class="pl " style="border-bottom: 0px;" valign="top"><a class="a" 
href="javascript:void(0);" onclick="top.Show.showAR( this, 'defref_us-
gaap_BasisOfPresentationAndSignificantAccountingPoliciesTextBlock', 
window );">BASIS OF PRESENTATION</a></td>
<td class="text"><p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt
0; text-align: justify"><b>NOTE 1.&#9;BASIS OF PRESENTATION</b></p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">In August 2009 the Company initiated a
number of corporate changes, including 1), a name change to TOA Distribution 
Systems Inc, (formerly known as Skyhigh Resources
Inc, 2) approved a 10 for 1 roll forward of its issued and outstanding common 
stock, 3), increased it authorized par value $0.001
common shares to 250,000,000 shares (formerly 50,000,000), and 4), authorized 
10,000,000 par value $0.001 preferred shares.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">In mid-2009, the Company resolved to change its corporate focus,
moving from mining and exploration into bottled drinking water distribution.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">The Company owned two (2) mineral properties acquired from related
parties in January 2008 by issuing stock to related parties. The purchase price 
was fully impaired. In February 2012 these claims
were deemed surplus and were sold in May 2012.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">On September 2, 2009 the Company entered into to a Sub-Distribution
agreement with Taste of Aruba (US), Inc to distribute bottled water products 
produced in Aruba by Taste of Aruba-Premium Aruban
Water. The territory in which the Company can distribute these products include 
the United States and all its territories and insular
areas in the Caribbean and Pacific such as but not limited to Puerto Rico, U.S. 
Virgin Islands, Marshall Islands, and Guam, and
all of Canada. In January 2016, the Company and Taste of Aruba agreed to cancel 
the Sub-Distribution agreement on a no loss no
gain basis for either party. Taste of Aruba was unable to confirm when its 
products would be available for resale. The 17,000,000
shares issued to cover the cost of the Sub-Distribution Agreement have been 
returned and were cancelled on January18, 2016. This
transaction which included full impairment has been reversed in the financial 
records for the year ended March 31, 2016.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">In the opinion of management, the accompanying balance sheets
and related statements of income, cash flows, and stockholders' equity include 
all adjustments, consisting only of normal recurring
items, necessary for their fair presentation in conformity with accounting 
principles generally accepted in the United States of
America (&#34;U.S. GAAP&#34;). Preparing financial statements requires 
management to make estimates and assumptions that affect
the reported amounts of assets, liabilities, revenue, and expenses. Actual 
results and outcomes may differ from management's estimates
and assumptions<b>. </b></p><span></span>
</td>
</tr>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">The accompanying financial statements have
been prepared in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP)
in the United States of America, which contemplates
continuation of the Company as a going concern. &#160;However, the Company has 
no business operations to date, accumulated losses
amounting to $174,401 and must secure additional financing to commence the 
Company&#146;s plan of operations, which means there
is substantial concern about the Company&#146;s ability to continue as a going 
concern. &#160;The Company intends to acquire additional
operating capital through equity offerings to the public to fund its business 
plan or loans from shareholders and others. There
is no assurance that the equity offerings will be successful or loans will be 
received to provide sufficient funds to commence
operations or to assure the eventual profitability of the Company.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p><span></span>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">Loans payable to related parties, were
received from a director of the Company and others closely associated persons or
businesses. These funds were provided as cash
loans to cover operating expenses and as payment for services provided.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">Loans payable to the past and current presidents
totaled $6,214 made up of principal amounting to $3,742 and accrued interest of 
$2,472</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">Loans payable to a closely associated business
totaled 88,937 made up of principal amounting to $75,498 and accrued interest 
amounting to $13,439.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">In aggregate, Loans Payable Related Parties
to June 30, 2016 totaled $95,151 made up of $79,240 for principal and $15,911 
for accrued interest.</p><span></span>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

7.&#9;EQUITY </b></p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; 
text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">At a special shareholders meeting held
August 13, 2009, the shareholders approved the change of the Company&#146;s name
to TOA Distribution Systems Inc, approved charges
to the authorized capital which included creation of 10,000,000 shares of 
preferred stock at a par value of $0.01 per share and
increased the authorized common stock to 250,000,000 with a par value of $0.001 
per share. As well, the shareholders approved a
10 for 1 forward stock split of the outstanding shares. All share amounts shown 
in these financial statements have been adjusted
retroactively to account for the forward stock split.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">At June 30, 2016 we had zero preferred
stock issued and outstanding and had 30,100,060 common shares issued and 
outstanding, which were issued on the dates and purposes
listed below.</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify; text-indent: 0.25in">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify; text-indent: 0.25in">- 15,000,000 common
shares issued to a director for cash at $0.0001 on December 13, 2007</p>

shares issued for a mining property at $0.01 on January10, 2007</p>

<td class="text"><p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt
0; text-align: justify"><b>NOTE 8.&#9;CONTRIBUTED SURPLUS</b></p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: 
justify">The Company owned two (2) mineral claims that had been deemed
surplus and fully impaired. On May 1, 2012 these claims were sold to a related 
party to whom the Company had loans payable. The
terms of the sale was a reduction of the loans payable and proportionate accrued
interest in aggregate amounting to Twenty-Five
Thousand Dollar, ($25,000.00), an extension on the due date of these loan 
payable, a reduction of the rate of interest payable
from 10% to 5% and the issuance by the purchaser, of shares in its two private 
companies. The Company elected to distribute these
private company shares equally to the Company&#146;s shareholders. As these 
shares were valued at $0 by the Company there was
no impact on the financial statements.</p><span></span>

<SEQUENCE>30
<FILENAME>Show.js
<DESCRIPTION>IDEA: XBRL DOCUMENT
<TEXT>
/**
 * Rivet Software Inc.
 *
 * @copyright Copyright (c) 2006-2011 Rivet Software, Inc. All rights reserved.
 * Version 2.4.0.3
 *
 */
var Show = {};
Show.LastAR = null,
Show.hideAR = function(){
Show.LastAR.style.display = 'none';
};
Show.showAR = function ( link, id, win ){
if( Show.LastAR ){
Show.hideAR();
}
var ref = link;
do {
ref = ref.nextSibling;
} while (ref && ref.nodeName != 'TABLE');
if (!ref || ref.nodeName != 'TABLE') {
var tmp = win ?
win.document.getElementById(id) :
document.getElementById(id);
if( tmp ){
ref = tmp.cloneNode(true);
ref.id = '';
link.parentNode.appendChild(ref);
}
}
if( ref ){
ref.style.display = 'block';
Show.LastAR = ref;
}
};
Show.toggleNext = function( link ){
var ref = link;
do{
ref = ref.nextSibling;
}while( ref.nodeName != 'DIV' );
if( ref.style &&
ref.style.display &&
ref.style.display == 'none' ){
ref.style.display = 'block';
if( link.textContent ){
link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '+', '-' );
}else{
link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '+', '-' );
}
}else{
ref.style.display = 'none';
if( link.textContent ){
link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '-', '+' );
}else{
link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '-', '+' );
}
}
};
</TEXT>
</DOCUMENT>
